### [1] [Resolved Maps of Gas and Dust in a Massive Quiescent Galaxy at z=2 from INQUEST-JWST: Evidence of Accretion and Rejuvenation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26195)
*Sai Gangula,Andrew B. Newman,Meng Gu,Sirio Belli,Katherine E. Whitaker,Tania M. Barone,Aliza Beverage,Andrea Bolamperti,Letizia Bugiani,Richard S. Ellis,Mariska Kriek,Allison Matthews,Themiya Nanayakkara*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 该论文利用JWST/NIRSpec IFU通过Na I D吸收线直接追踪z=2宁静星系的中性气体运动学，为研究早期宁静星系的气体吸积与再活跃提供了迄今最清晰的观测证据，对你的高红移星系演化研究有直接的方法学启示和物理机制参考。

TL;DR: 利用JWST/NIRSpec IFU对红移约2的引力透镜现象星系MRG-M0138进行观测，通过Na I D吸收线追踪中性气体的分布与运动学，发现气体与恒星盘共转、存在非平衡结构（如离核团块、尘埃带），结合恒星形成历史揭示500 Myr前的再活跃事件，表明气体来自潮汐吸积，并解释了早期宁静星系气体含量差异的原因及AGN反馈燃料机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 遥远宇宙中的宁静星系具有不同的气体含量，暗示多种熄灭机制在起作用，但此前对气体分布和运动学的观测几乎都是未分辨的，因此需要高空间分辨率的观测来追溯气体起源。

Method: 使用JWST/NIRSpec IFU对引力透镜星系MRG-M0138进行观测，在219个空间分块中利用Na I D吸收线（扣除恒星吸收后）追踪中性气体的运动学和空间分布。

Result: 气体呈现清晰的旋转运动，且与恒星盘运动学对齐；气体和尘埃具有复杂的空间结构，包括离核团块、尘埃带和外盘斑块；非平衡分布表明气体是吸积而来的；恒星形成历史分析显示500 Myr前存在再活跃事件；识别出两个可能相关的伴星系；在距离已知超大质量黑洞约90 pc处探测到气体团块。

Conclusion: 早期宁静星系的气体含量差异并非完全由气体消耗时标不同导致；潮汐相互作用是气体吸积的可能来源；探测到靠近超大质量黑洞的气体团块为间歇性AGN反馈提供燃料机制，有助于维持星系的宁静状态。

Abstract: Quiescent galaxies in the distant universe exhibit a range of gas content that may indicate a variety of quenching processes are at play. Mapping the distribution and kinematics of the gas can illuminate its origins, but nearly all such observations have been unresolved. We present JWST/NIRSpec IFU observations of MRG-M0138, a gravitationally lensed, massive quiescent galaxy at $z\sim2$ observed as part of the INQUEST-JWST survey. We use Na I D absorption, which we detect in excess of the stellar absorption over most of the galaxy, to trace the kinematics and spatial distribution of the neutral gas in 219 spatial bins. The gas exhibits clear rotation that is kinematically aligned with the stellar disk. Both the gas and dust have a complex spatial structure, including an off-nuclear clump, a dust lane, and patches in the outer disk. The non-equilibrium distribution suggests that the gas was accreted. Analysis of the galaxy's star formation history supports this interpretation by indicating a rejuvenation event 500 Myrs ago. We identify two plausibly associated galaxies and suggest that tidal interactions are a likely source of the accreted gas. Our results indicate that some of the variation in gas content among early quiescent galaxies is not related to differences in gas consumption timescales. The detection of a gas clump at a projected distance of $\sim90$ pc from the known supermassive black hole illustrates a mechanism to fuel the episodic AGN feedback that may maintain quiescence.

</details>


### [2] [The ALMA-QUARKS Survey: Evidence of an Explosive Molecular Outflow in IRAS 15520--5234](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15040)
*Ariful Hoque,Tapas Baug,Estrella Guzman,Manuel Fernandez Lopez,Tie Liu,Guido Garay,Paul F. Goldsmith,Fengwei Xu,Xindi Tang,Patricio Sanhueza,Lokesh K. Dewangan,Shivani Gupta,Sami Dib,Luis A. Zapata,Jihye Hwang,N. K. Bhadari,John Bally,Swagat Ranjan Das,Aiyuan Yang,Prasanta Gorai,Arup Kumar Maity,James O. Chibueze,Pablo García,Leonardo Bronfman,Xunchuan Liu,L. Viktor Tóth,Shehu Muhammad Usman,Kee-Tae Kim*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 该论文通过ALMA高分辨率观测揭示了爆炸性分子外流的动力学特征（哈勃-勒梅特定律），并给出了精确的年龄和发生率估计，为研究大质量恒星形成中的爆发性事件提供了关键观测约束和动力学模型验证。

TL;DR: 本文研究了IRAS 15520-5234大质量原星团，发现其具有爆炸性分子外流特征，释放至少10^48尔格动能，包含16个致密核和28个准直外流指状结构，符合哈勃-勒梅特定律，无特定取向，年龄约6550年，银河系中此类事件约每83年发生一次。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究大质量原星团IRAS 15520-5234中的爆炸性分子外流现象，探索其物理特性、能量释放规模、形成机制以及在银河系中的发生频率。

Method: 使用ALMA波段6连续谱发射图探测16个致密核，分析CO(2-1)发射线揭示28个准直外流指状结构，通过哈勃-勒梅特定律分析运动学特征，计算外流的总质量、动量和动能，估算动力学年龄和银河系发生频率。

Result: 发现爆炸性外流释放至少10^48尔格动能，外流指状结构无特定取向且源自共同中心，其质量、动量和动能比典型大质量原恒星双极外流高至少一个数量级，动力学年龄约6550年，银河系中此类事件约每83年发生一次。

Conclusion: IRAS 15520-5234的爆炸性外流特征表明其能量释放远超典型原恒星外流，可能是由原星团内质量重新分布和大质量核心间的动力学相互作用形成的，此类事件在银河系中相对频繁发生。

Abstract: We present a study of the massive protocluster IRAS 15520$-$5234, which displays evidence of an explosive molecular outflow that unleashed a kinetic energy of at least 10$^{48}$ erg. The protocluster contains 16 dense cores detected in the ALMA band 6 continuum emission maps, having masses in the range from 0.2 to 11.0 M$_{\odot}$. Our analysis of CO $(2-1)$ emission reveals 28 well collimated outflow fingers, the majority of which follow a Hubble-Lemaître velocity law. The outflow fingers show no preferred orientation in the plane of sky and emerge from a common center of origin. We estimate the total mass, momentum, and kinetic energy of the outflow fingers and find that the values are at least one order of magnitude higher than the typical bipolar outflows associated with massive protostars. The morphology and kinematics of the outflow fingers suggest that the outflow associated with IRAS 15520$-$5234 is explosive in nature. We calculate the dynamical age of the explosive event to be approximately 6550 years. Additionally, we estimate the frequency of such explosive outflows in the Galaxy, which is one event every 83 years. Finally, we speculate that the rearrangement of masses within the massive protocluster and the dynamical interaction among the massive cores may result in the formation of such an energetic event.

</details>


### [3] [Magnetic field morphological diagnostics with ALMA in the G327.29 protocluster: VGT versus dust polarization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.13473)
*A. Koley,A. M. Stutz,A. Lazarian,Y. Hu,P. Sanhueza,P. Saha,R. H. Alvarez-Gutierrez,N. S. Sandoval-Garrido,N. Castro-Toledo,G. Bernal Mesina*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 该论文将VGT技术首次应用于大质量原星团的高分辨率ALMA观测，为你在星系尺度上研究湍流与磁场相互作用提供了可移植的诊断工具，尤其是对多相介质中速度梯度与偏振互验的方法论启发。

TL;DR: 本研究首次将速度梯度技术（VGT）应用于大质量原星团G327.29，结合分子线发射和尘埃偏振观测，揭示了该区域由湍流和重力共同塑造的复杂磁场结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁场和湍流在原星团演化中可能起关键作用，影响致密核和恒星的形成。研究旨在通过比较VGT和尘埃偏振，探索大质量恒星形成区域的演化过程。

Method: 使用ALMA 12米阵列观测四种分子示踪剂（DCN、C18O、HN13C、H13CO+）的分子线发射，提取速度梯度技术（VGT）分析磁场形态，并与尘埃连续谱发射的线性偏振观测结果进行比较。

Result: 揭示了G327.29原星团复杂的磁场结构，由湍流和重力共同塑造；发现存在从周围介质到纤维状结构和中心最密区域的大尺度引力坍缩；观测到核区由湍流和重力共同主导。

Conclusion: 本研究首次将VGT技术应用于大质量原星团G327.29的高分辨率ALMA观测，VGT与尘埃偏振的比较为探索大质量恒星形成区域的演化过程提供了有力工具。

Abstract: Magnetic fields and turbulence may play a key role in the evolution of protoclusters, influencing the formation of dense cores and stars. Here, we examine the morphology of the magnetic fields in the G327.29 protocluster using both the velocity gradient technique (VGT) extracted from molecular line emissions and linear polarization in the dust continuum emission. The VGT analysis is performed using four molecular tracers: DCN (3-2), C18O (2-1), HN13C (3-2), and H13CO+ (3-2) - which probe gas across different density regimes, observed with the ALMA 12 m array. Owing to its sensitivity to gas dynamics, a comparison between VGT and dust polarization provides a powerful probe of the evolutionary processes in massive star-forming regions. From our analysis we reveal a complex magnetic-field structure, shaped by the combined influence of turbulence and gravity. In addition, it also appears that there is a large-scale (beyond the core scale) gravitational infall from the surrounding medium on to the filament and the central densest region. Furthermore, we observe that cores are dominated by a mix of turbulence and gravity. Overall, this work presents, likely for the first time, the application of VGT to a massive protocluster, G327.29, using high-resolution ALMA observations.

</details>


### [4] [Molecular gas and star formation in central rings across nearby galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.11127)
*Damian R. Gleis,Sophia K. Stuber,Eva Schinnerer,Justus Neumann,Sharon E. Meidt,Miguel Querejeta,Eric Emsellem,Adam K. Leroy,Ashley T. Barnes,Frank Bigiel,Charlie Burton,Mélanie Chevance,Daniel A. Dale,Kathryn Grasha,Ralf S. Klessen,Rebecca C. Levy,Lukas Neumann,Hsi-An Pan,Marina Ruiz-García,Mattia C. Sormani,Jiayi Sun,Yu-Hsuan Teng,Thomas G. Williams*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 该论文通过高分辨率CO(2-1)观测直接对比银河系中央分子区与星系中心环的分子气体和恒星形成特性，为理解银河系与外部星系中棒旋驱动的气体聚集和星暴机制提供了统一的定量标尺。

TL;DR: 利用高分辨率CO(2-1)观测研究附近星系中心环的分子气体含量和恒星形成率，发现银河系中央分子区与这些中心环在相对参数上相似


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究附近星系中心环的分子气体含量和恒星形成率，并将其与银河系中央分子区(CMZ)进行比较，了解中心环的形成机制和演化过程

Method: 使用PHANGS-ALMA的1角秒分辨率CO(2-1)观测数据，视觉识别20个中心环，测量其几何形状、分子气体质量、恒星形成率、消耗时间等参数，并与宿主星系和棒状结构特性进行比较

Result: 中心环典型半径约400pc，分子气体质量约10^8.1太阳质量，恒星形成率约0.21太阳质量/年，贡献宿主星系分子气体质量的5.6%和恒星形成率的13%；银河系CMZ处于分布的低端但相对参数相似；较长棒状结构包含更高质量的中心环

Conclusion: 尽管绝对参数可能依赖于宿主星系特性，但银河系CMZ与PHANGS中心环在相对参数上的相似性表明，附近星系中心环的气体流入和恒星形成过程是相似的

Abstract: Nearby galaxies exhibit a variety of structures, including central rings, similar to the MW Central Molecular Zone (CMZ). These rings are common in barred galaxies and can be gas-rich and highly star-forming. We aim to study molecular gas content and star formation rate of central rings within nearby galaxies and link them to global galaxy properties (e.g. bar morphology). We utilize $1\,$'' resolution CO(2-1) PHANGS-ALMA observations, visually identify 20 central rings and determine their properties. For $14$ rings, SFR surface density maps are available. We derive ring geometry, integrated molecular gas masses, SFRs, depletion times, and compare them to host galaxy and bar properties. Molecular gas is a good tracer for central rings: Previous studies used ionized gas and dust tracers to identify central rings in galaxies of similar morphological types as this study. In comparison, we find similar fractions of galaxies hosting central rings and similar radii distributions. The gaseous central rings have typical radii of $400_{-150}^{+250}\,$pc, molecular gas masses of $\log(M_\text{mol}/M_\odot){\sim}8.1_{-0.23}^{+0.17}$, and SFRs of $0.21_{-0.16}^{+0.15}\,M_\odot/\text{yr}$, thus contributing $5.6_{-2.1}^{+4.5}\,\%$ and $13_{-5}^{+10}\,\%$ to their host galaxies' molecular gas mass and SFR. The MW CMZ sits at the lower end of the radius, molecular gas mass, and SFR distribution, but it has a similar molecular gas mass and SFR fraction, and depletion time. Longer bars contain more massive molecular central rings, but we find no correlation between bar strength and the ring's molecular gas content. Although absolute central ring properties likely depend on host galaxy properties, the similarities between the MW CMZ and PHANGS central rings in relative parameters suggest that the processes of gas inflow and star formation are similar for central rings across nearby galaxies.

</details>


### [5] [An Active Galaxy Cluster Merger at Cosmic Noon Revealed by JWST Weak Lensing and Multiwavelength Probes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.11022)
*Zachary P. Scofield,Kyle Finner,Hyungjin Joo,M. James Jee,Wonki Lee,Sangjun Cha,Jinhyub Kim,Yu-Heng Lin,Ranga-Ram Chary,Andreas Faisst,Bomee Lee*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 本文通过JWST弱引力透镜首次在宇宙正午时期直接描绘出星系团合并的质量图，为利用高红移多波段数据约束暗物质和重子物质碰撞行为提供了新观测基准。

TL;DR: JWST观测揭示了一个罕见的高红移星系团XLSSC 122，其质量分布与X射线、SZ效应等多波段数据一致，显示出明显的合并活动特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高红移（z=1.98）星系团XLSSC 122的质量分布和演化状态，探索宇宙早期星系团的组装过程。

Method: 利用JWST/NIRCam深度成像进行弱引力透镜分析，重建星系团质量分布；结合Chandra X射线数据、MeerKAT射电成像、ALMA/ACA/ACT SZ效应测量以及JWST星系团内光测量进行多波段综合分析。

Result: 测得质量M200c=1.6±0.3×10¹⁴ M⊙，浓度c200c=6.3±0.3，与强透镜估计一致；发现质量峰与X射线峰、最亮星系位置重合；多波段数据显示一致的NE-SW方向拉长，SZ峰与质量/X射线峰存在显著偏移，表明存在显著的合并活动。

Conclusion: XLSSC 122作为JWST高红移透镜研究的试点，证明了JWST在z~2处测绘星系团质量分布的独特能力，为研究宇宙正午时期的星系团组装提供了重要案例。

Abstract: The galaxy cluster XLSSC 122 is a rare system at $z = 1.98$, hosting surprisingly evolved member galaxies when the Universe was only one-third of its present age. Leveraging deep JWST/NIRCam imaging, we perform a weak-lensing analysis and reconstruct the cluster's mass distribution, finding a mass peak that coincides with both the X-ray peak and the position of the brightest cluster galaxy. We obtain mass and concentration estimates of $M_{200\rm c}=1.6 \pm 0.3\times 10^{14}~M_{\odot}$ and $c_{200 \rm c}=6.3 \pm 0.3$, respectively, in agreement with recent strong-lensing estimates. The high concentration in particular motivates tests against empirical and simulation-derived mass--concentration relations. Placing our weak-lensing mass map in the context of Chandra X-ray data, MeerKAT radio imaging, ALMA+ACA/ACT Sunyaev-Zel'dovich (SZ) mapping, and a new JWST intracluster light measurement, we identify consistent NE--SW elongation across datasets and a pronounced offset along the same axis between the SZ and mass/X-ray peaks, pointing to significant merger activity. XLSSC 122 thus serves as a JWST pilot study for high-$z$ lensing, demonstrating the telescope's unique ability to map cluster mass distributions at $z\sim2$ and motivating a uniform sample of analogous systems with joint lensing, X-ray, SZ, and radio data to probe cluster assembly at Cosmic Noon.

</details>


### [6] [Direct detection of cool molecular gas in a star-forming galaxy at $z=7.31$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13393)
*Karin Cescon,Jacqueline A. Hodge,Leindert A. Boogaard,Hiddo S. B. Algera,Lucie E. Rowland,Dominik A. Riechers,Renske Smit,Ilse De Looze,Rychard Bouwens,Paul van der Werf,Manuel Aravena,Elisabete da Cunha,Pratika Dayal,Andrea Ferrara,Rebecca Fisher,Hanae Inami,Pavel E. Mancera Piña,Pascal A. Oesch,Andrea Pallottini,Matus Rybak,Sander Schouws,Laura Sommovigo,Mauro Stefanon,Livia Vallini*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (85/100) - 该研究直接探测到z>7星系的CO发射线，并验证了[C II]作为早期宇宙分子气体示踪剂的可行性，为你利用ALMA开展再电离时期星系分子气体含量与恒星形成效率的研究提供了关键的方法学验证和观测模板。

TL;DR: 该研究通过探测z=7.31星系REBELS-25的CO(3-2)和CO(7-6)发射线，确认了宇宙大爆炸后仅7亿年就存在一个极端巨大的分子气体库（约10¹¹ M☉），气体分数高达95%，并验证了[C II]作为早期宇宙分子气体示踪剂的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探索早期宇宙（再电离时代）星系的分子气体含量和星际介质条件，以理解星系在宇宙最初十亿年内的快速质量积累过程。

Method: 利用VLA Q波段和ALMA Band 3观测CO(3-2)和CO(7-6)发射线，结合辐射传输代码TUNER自洽建模CO和尘埃连续谱发射，并考虑宇宙微波背景（CMB）的影响。

Result: 探测到CO(3-2)和CO(7-6)发射（均约3.5σ），获得分子气体质量约1.0×10¹¹ M☉（依赖α_CO假设）或1.8×10¹¹ M☉（通过TUNER建模），气体分数约0.95，气体尘埃比约600，消耗时标约1.2 Gyr，并推导出[C II]-H₂转换因子为60±25 M☉/L☉。

Conclusion: 该工作直接证实了z>7星系中低J CO发射的可探测性，为下一代观测设施铺平道路，并表明[C II]在再电离时代仍是可行的分子气体示踪剂，揭示了早期星系快速质量积累的关键信息。

Abstract: We investigate the molecular gas content and interstellar medium (ISM) conditions of REBELS-25, a massive, star-forming galaxy at $z=7.31$. Deep VLA Q-band and ALMA Band 3 observations reveal CO(3-2) and CO(7-6) emission (both at $\sim3.5σ$), and provide an upper limit on [C I](2-1). From the CMB-corrected CO(3-2) flux-representing the highest-redshift detection of a low-$J$ CO transition to date-we derive a molecular gas mass of $M_{\rm mol}=(1.0\pm0.4)\times10^{11}\,(α_{\rm CO}/(3\,$M$_{\odot}$(K$\,$\kms$\,$pc$^2)^{-1}))\,$M$_{\odot}$, directly confirming the presence of a very massive gas reservoir only $\simeq700\,$Myr after the Big Bang. This implies an extreme gas fraction of $f_{\rm gas}\simeq0.95$, a gas-to-dust ratio of $δ_{\rm GDR}\simeq6\times10^2$, and a depletion timescale of $τ_{\rm dep}\simeq1.2\,$Gyr, broadly consistent with extrapolated scaling relations for main-sequence galaxies at lower redshift. Using the radiative transfer code TUNER, we self-consistently model CO and dust continuum emission in the context of the significant CMB background, constraining ISM properties and recovering $M_{\rm mol}= (1.8^{+1.0}_{-0.9})\times10^{11}\,$M$_{\odot}$, independent of assumptions about $r_{31}$ and $α_{\rm CO}$. We further discuss the use of alternative molecular gas tracers at early epochs. Combining CO and [C II] measurements, we infer an empirical [C II]-to-H$_2$ conversion factor of $α_{\rm [C II]}=(60\pm25)\,$M$_{\odot}$/L$_{\odot}$, suggesting [C II] remains a viable molecular gas tracer in the Epoch of Reionization. These results demonstrate the detectability of low-$J$ CO emission even at $z>7$, paving the way for next-generation facilities, and provide critical insights into the rapid mass assembly of galaxies during the first billion years of cosmic history.

</details>


### [7] [Molecular Gas Structure and Star Formation Diversity in Stephan's Quintet Revealed by ACA CO(1-0) Mapping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10557)
*Misaki Yamamoto,Fumiya Maeda,Kazuyuki Muraoka,Fumi Egusa,Shinya Komugi,Bunyo Hatsukade,Hiroyuki Kaneko,Masato I. N. Kobayashi,Kotaro Kohno,Ayu Konishi,Kana Morokuma-Matsui,Kouichiro Nakanishi,Kouji Ohta*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (85/100) - 该论文首次利用ACA对致密星系群进行大尺度高分辨率CO(1-0)成像，直接揭示了潮汐尾分子团块及湍流与恒星形成效率的反相关，为你的相互作用星系物理和恒星形成反馈研究提供了关键的观测证据和新的分析视角。

TL;DR: 本文利用ALMA阿塔卡马紧凑阵列对斯蒂芬五重星系（一个著名的致密星系群）进行了首次大尺度、高空间分辨率的$^{12}$CO(1-0)分子气体成像，揭示了分子气体主要分布在成员星系NGC 7319的盘面及星系际空间，并发现了沿潮汐尾分布的四个CO团块；结合H$α$数据发现恒星形成效率与CO速度弥散呈负相关，表明湍流在相互作用的星系系统中对恒星形成起重要调控作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 致密星系群中的星际介质相互作用和恒星形成调控机制尚不明确，缺乏大尺度、高分辨率的分子气体观测数据来揭示其物理过程。

Method: 利用ALMA的7米阵列加总功率观测进行$^{12}$CO(1-0)分子气体成像，结合H$α$和H I等多波段数据，分析分子气体分布、团块性质以及恒星形成效率与速度弥散的关系。

Result: 获得了137 kpc×119 kpc、分辨率约5.5 kpc的分子气体图；发现四个离散CO团块（速度弥散10-30 km/s，质量10⁷-10⁸ M☉）；恒星形成效率跨度约2.2 dex（0.02-4 Gyr⁻¹），与CO速度弥散呈负相关。

Conclusion: 湍流在相互作用星系系统中对恒星形成起重要的调控作用，高湍流区域（如激波丝附近）的恒星形成被强烈抑制。

Abstract: We present $^{12}$CO(1-0) mapping across the entire system of Stephan's Quintet, a well-known compact galaxy group, observed by Atacama Compact Array (7\,m array + Total Power) of the Atacama Large Millimeter/submillimeter Array. These observations provide the first large-scale ($137\,\mathrm{kpc}\times119\,\mathrm{kpc}$), spatially resolved ($\sim$5.5\,$\mathrm{kpc}$) molecular gas map of a compact group. Our CO map revealed that most of the molecular gas resides in the disk of the member galaxy NGC~7319 and in the intergalactic regions, including components along the shocked filament and the optically identified tidal tail extending from NGC~7319. Along the tidal tail and its surroundings, we found not only an extended molecular gas component but also four discrete CO clumps, with velocity dispersions of $\sim$10-30 $\mathrm{km\,s^{-1}}$ and molecular gas masses of order $10^7$-$10^8\,M_\odot$. Three of these clumps spatially overlap with H\,{\sc i}, whereas the remaining clump shows no associated H\,{\sc i} or counterparts at optical and infrared wavelengths. Using star formation rates derived from H$α$ luminosities of H\,{\sc ii} regions, we found that star formation efficiencies (SFEs) span $\sim$2.2\,dex ($\sim$0.02--4\,Gyr$^{-1}$) and negatively correlate with CO velocity dispersion. While regions with small velocity dispersion exhibit SFEs comparable to those of nearby disk galaxies, those with large velocity dispersion ($\sim$50-150$\,\mathrm{km\,s^{-1}}$) around the shocked filament show strongly suppressed star formation. These results suggest that turbulence plays a significant role in regulating star formation in interacting systems.

### [8] [Dust in the very metal-poor galaxy Sextans A with JWST. I: Characterizing the evolved stellar population of Sextans A based on JWST observations and stellar evolution models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07421)
*C. Gavetti,F. Dell'Agli,E. Tarantino,M. L. Boyer,I. McDonald,J. Th. Van Loon,D. A. Garcia-Hernandez,M. A. T. Groenewegen,A. Nanni,J. A. D. L. Blommaert,R. D. Gehrz,L. M. Gerlach,S. Goldman,M. Recommendation: ★★★★★ (85/100) - 本文通过JWST近中红外数据首次在超低金属丰度（约1-7%太阳丰度）矮星系中系统表征AGB恒星的尘埃产生率，为你的研究提供了低金属丰度环境下恒星演化与尘埃形成耦合的直接观测约束。

TL;DR: 本研究利用JWST对超低金属丰度（约1-7%太阳丰度）的矮星系Sextans A进行1-21微米成像，分析了其渐近巨星分支（AGB）恒星的特性。研究发现超过90%的AGB恒星呈现几乎垂直的色-星等序列，缺乏星周尘；少量强红外超源为碳星，起源于约2-3 Gyr前形成的1.25-1.5 Msun前身星。JWST/NIRCam F277W-F444W颜色可作为尘埃产生率的有效指标，最红源预测尘埃产生率可达10^-7 Msun/年。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Sextans A作为极低金属丰度（约1-7%太阳丰度）的近邻恒星形成矮星系，为研究早期宇宙星系演化提供了独特窗口。利用JWST在1-21微米波段的成像数据，可详细表征其尘埃恒星种群和星际介质特性，特别是AGB恒星的尘埃产生过程。

Method: 将JWST观测到的AGB恒星色-星等分布与恒星演化和尘埃形成模型进行对比分析。使用0.8-7 Msun、金属丰度Z=10^-3的演化轨迹，结合NIRCam和MIRI多波段测光数据，分析AGB种群的前身星质量、形成时代、金属丰度和尘埃产生特性。

Result: 1) 超过90%的AGB恒星呈现几乎垂直的色-星等序列，主要为贫氧（M型）AGB星，缺少星周尘，F444W波段可作为可靠的亮度诊断指标。2) 少量强红外超源为碳星，起源于约2-3 Gyr前形成的1.25-1.5 Msun前身星，处于AGB末期，金属丰度约1-2%太阳丰度。3) F277W-F444W颜色可作为尘埃产生率的有效代理指标。

Conclusion: JWST对Sextans A的观测揭示了极低金属丰度环境下AGB恒星种群的特征，证实了大多数AGB星缺乏尘埃包裹，而少量碳星贡献主要尘埃产出。F277W-F444W颜色可作为有效的尘埃产生率诊断工具，为理解早期宇宙尘埃形成和星系演化提供了重要参考。

Abstract: The nearby star-forming dwarf galaxy Sextans A offers a unique window into galaxy evolution in the early Universe, owing to its extremely low metallicity (about 1-7% Zsun). Recent JWST imaging of Sextans A spanning 1-21 micron enables a detailed characterization of its dusty stellar populations and interstellar medium. In this work, we compare the observed JWST color-magnitude distributions of evolved stars with stellar evolution and dust-formation models to characterize the properties of the asymptotic giant branch (AGB) population, including progenitor mass, formation epoch, metallicity, and dust production. Evolutionary tracks for 0.8-7 Msun stars with metallicity Z=10^-3 provide good agreement with the overall distribution of AGB stars in Sextans A. More than 90% of the AGB population occupies a nearly vertical sequence in the color-magnitude diagrams, corresponding to stars spanning a wide range of masses and ages but exhibiting little or no circumstellar dust. This sequence appears to be dominated by oxygen-rich (M-type) AGB stars and reveals that the F444W flux is a robust luminosity diagnostic. A small subset of sources displays strong infrared excesses and is dominated by carbon stars descending from 1.25-1.5 Msun progenitors that formed about 2-3 Gyr ago and are currently in the final AGB phases. Their MIRI colors imply very low metallicities, consistent with estimates from the red giant branch morphology (about 1-2% Zsun). Finally, we show that the JWST/NIRCam F277W-F444W color serves as an effective proxy for the dust production rate, with models predicting rates up to 10^-7 Msun/yr for the reddest sources in Sextans A.

### [9] [The Multi-phase Biconical Outflow in the local IR-Luminous Merger IRASF01364-1042](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06005)
*Y. Song,V. U,J. Kader,M. Bianchin,J. Agostino,L. Barcos-Muñoz,N. Torres-Albà,A. Medling,C. Ricci,L. Armus,T. Lai,L. Ghodsi,A. Evans,H. Inami,S. Stierwalt,T. Bohn,K. L. Emig,V. Buiten,G. Donnelly,E. Treister,A. Jimenez-Gallardo,T. Böker,D. Kakkad,S. Linden,P. van der Werf,V. Charmandaris,R. Remigio,L. Lenkic,C. Finlez,M. Sanchez-García,C. Lofaro,A. Saravia,I. Yoon,G. C. Privon,T. Gao,H. Aziz,R. McGurk,T. Díaz-Santos,D. Kunneriath,David B. Sanders*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (85/100) - 该研究通过多波段IFU数据首次在单个源中分离出AGN与星暴对外流的贡献，这为你处理类似存在严重尘埃遮蔽的并合星系中多相外流驱动机制时，提供了可借鉴的诊断线组合与动力学建模方法。

TL;DR: 利用JWST、ALMA和Keck的多波段IFU观测，研究了局部红外亮星系并合体IRAS F01364-1042的空间分辨ISM特性。确认存在多相星系双锥状外流，其中冷分子相主导质量外流率和动能。首次通过[Ne V]线检测到尘埃遮蔽的AGN，但核星暴足以驱动外流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解并合驱动尘埃星暴星系的星际介质特性、多相气体外流动力学，以及探测其中可能存在的遮蔽低光度AGN。

Method: 结合JWST/MIRI-MRS、ALMA和Keck/KCWI的多波段IFU观测，构建电离气体、暖分子和冷分子气体发射线图，并对分辨区域的光谱进行详细分解。

Result: 确认多相双锥状外流，电离相、暖分子相和冷分子相外流速度分别约500-600、~350和200-300 km/s，质量外流率分别约0.3-2.3、~31和38-240 M☉/yr。冷分子相主导总质量外流率和动能(~2-8×10^42 erg/s)。首次通过[Ne V]线探测到尘埃遮蔽AGN，其辐射热光度约1.2-1.8×10^43 erg/s。

Conclusion: 核星暴（SFR约40-60 M☉/yr）足以提供驱动外流所需的能量，尽管近期更活跃的AGN也可能起过作用。多波段观测对解析并合驱动尘埃星暴星系的气体动力学至关重要，JWST/MIRI-MRS有能力揭示其中常见的遮蔽低光度AGN。

Abstract: We investigate the spatially-resolved ISM properties of the local ($z = 0.048$), IR-luminous ($L_{\rm IR} = 10^{11.87}$\,L$_\odot$), late-stage galaxy merger IRAS F01364-1042, combining multi-wavelength IFU observations from \textit{JWST/MIRI-MRS}, ALMA and Keck/KCWI. Using these datasets, we construct emission line maps of several key tracers of the ionized (e.g., [Ne\,II]\,12.8$μ$m, [O\,III]$\lambda5007$), warm molecular (e.g., \ce{H2}\,0-0\,S(3)), and cold molecular gas (e.g., CO (J$=2-1$)), and perform detailed decomposition of spectra extracted in resolved regions across the areas of emission. We confirm the presence of a multi-phase galactic biconical outflow along the minor axis of a highly inclined rotating disk. The inferred outflow velocities are $\sim\,$500 - 600\,km\,s$^{-1}$ $\sim\,$350\,km\,s$^{-1}$, and $\sim\,$200 - 300\,km\,s$^{-1}$, in the ionized, warm and cold molecular phase, respectively, with corresponding mass outflow rates of $\sim 0.3 - 2.3$, $\sim 31$, and $\sim 38 - 240$\,M$_\odot\,$yr$^{-1}$. The cold molecular phase dominates both the total mass outflow rate and the associated kinetic energy ($\sim\,2 - 8 \times 10^{42}$\,erg\,s$^{-1}$). We confirm, for the first time, a dust-obscured AGN in IRAS\,F01364-1042, via detection of the [Ne\,V]\,14.3$μ$m line. The low inferred AGN bolometric luminosity ($1.2 - 1.8 \times 10^{43}$\,erg\,s$^{-1}$) suggests that the nuclear starburst alone, with a star formation rate of $\sim 40 - 60$\,M$_\odot$\,yr$^{-1}$, can account for the energy required to drive the outflow, though a more active AGN phase in the recent past may have also played a role. Our work showcases the necessity of multi-wavelength observations for interpreting the gas dynamics in merger-driven dusty starbursts, and the capability of \textit{JWST/MIRI-MRS} to uncover obscured, low-luminosity AGN that may be common in these systems.

### [10] [Strong environmental AGN enhancement among DSFGs in z > 2 protoclusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05283)
*Monica Natalia Isla Llave,Fabio Vito,Alberto Traina,Cristian Vignali,Olga Cucciati,Benjamin Forrest,Gayathri Gururajan,Brian Lemaux,Sylvia Adscheid,Sebastiano Cantalupo,Kazuki Daikuhara,Marta Galbiati,Roberto Gilli,Tadayuki Kodama,Stefano Marchesi,Maurillio Pannella,Antonio Pensabene,Maria del Carmen Polletta,Rhythm Shimakawa,Paolo Tozzi*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (85/100) - 该研究首次系统量化了高红移原星团环境中尘埃星暴星系AGN的比例增强，为理解超大质量黑洞在星系团致密形成阶段与恒星形成活动协同增长的环境驱动机制提供了关键观测约束，对你正在进行的星系环境效应研究有直接的方法论借鉴。

TL;DR: 该研究通过对比7个高红移（2<z<4.5）星系原星团与宇宙场中的尘埃星暴星系，发现原星团环境中的X射线AGN比例显著提高约2.7倍，表明密集环境通过增强气体供应和相互作用促进了超大质量黑洞的增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究因星系样本选择和AGN识别方法不统一，导致对星系原星团环境如何影响超大质量黑洞增长这一问题缺乏清晰认识。

Method: 利用ALMA探测的7个星系原星团（2<z<4.5）中的尘埃星暴星系，构建与COSMOS巡天匹配的对照样本，通过均匀的能谱分布拟合比较X射线AGN发生率及宿主星系物理性质。

Result: 原星团中X射线AGN比例比场样本高约2.7倍（显著性p=3e-4），在红移2-3和3-4.5两个区间分别约为2.7倍（p=0.003）和2.6倍（p=0.03）。两组样本在恒星质量、恒星形成率和尘埃质量上匹配良好，排除选择效应或质量差异的驱动。

Conclusion: 密集星系原星团环境显著增强了尘埃星暴星系中的AGN活动，推动了超大质量黑洞的增长，这一效应独立于宿主星系本身的性质，很可能通过增加气体可用性和相互作用驱动的物质吸积实现。

Abstract: Galaxy protoclusters (PCs) at z > 2 are dense regions in which cold gas availability and elevated galaxy interaction rates trigger intense, often dust-obscured, star formation. These mechanisms are also expected to promote super-massive black hole (SMBH) growth, but this effect remains unclear, largely due to heterogeneous galaxy selections and active galactic nuclei (AGN) identification methods in previous studies. We quantitatively assess the impact of PC environment on SMBH growth by measuring the incidence of X-ray AGN among dusty star-forming galaxies (DSFGs) in PCs and in a homogeneously selected control field sample, and investigate the physical mechanisms driving any difference. We consider ALMA-detected DSFGs in sub-mm/mm continuum of seven PCs at 2 < z < 4.5, and construct a selection-matched control sample from the COSMOS survey. We statistically compare X-ray AGN incidence and host galaxy physical properties obtained through uniform spectral energy distribution fitting. We find a significant enhancement of X-ray AGN fraction in PCs by ~2.7x (Poisson significance p = 3e-4). Similar values are found in two redshift bins: ~2.7x at z = 2-3 (p = 0.003) and ~2.6x at z = 3-4.5 (p = 0.03). PC and field DSFG samples are well matched in stellar mass, star-formation rate, and dust mass, ruling out selection effects or systematically higher host masses as the driver. Our results provide quantitative evidence that the dense PC environment enhances AGN incidence and SMBH growth in DSFGs beyond what host galaxy properties alone predict, likely through increased gas availability and interaction-driven fueling. This work is a first step toward a homogeneous assessment of environmental effects on SMBH growth across cosmic time.

### [11] [NISER-IUCAA New Simulations of JWST GAlaxies and Quasars(NINJA): Properties of galaxies at $5 \leq z \leq 10$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26211)
*Ranit Behera,Raghunathan Srianand,Nishikanta Khandai,Prakash Gaikwad*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (85/100) - 该NINJA模拟套件直接针对JWST高红移观测，通过调整尘埃模型复现UV光度函数，对你未来利用JWST数据约束星系形成模型有直接的参数化指导意义。

TL;DR: 本文介绍了NINJA宇宙学流体动力学模拟套件，研究了JWST时代z≥5的星系形成与演化。通过调整光谱合成模型和尘埃衰减参数，可重现5≤z≤10的观测UV光度函数，但模型之间存在显著差异，需要多观测约束来限制高红移尘埃模型。在z≥10时，模型低估了UVLF，表明需要更高分辨率的模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了在JWST时代研究高红移（z≥5）星系的形成与演化，需要能够重现观测结果的宇宙学模拟工具，同时探究尘埃模型、反馈机制等关键物理过程对模拟结果的影响。

Method: 使用NINJA宇宙学流体动力学模拟套件，结合不同的光谱合成模型和尘埃衰减模型，调整参数以匹配5≤z≤10的观测UVLF，并比较多种观测量的预测结果。

Result: 适当参数可以重现5≤z≤10的UVLF；尘埃-金属比随红移演化，但归一化因子在不同模型间变化约7倍；不同模型在B波段LF、Hα LF、UV斜率-星等相关关系等预测上存在显著散射；在z≥10时模型低估了UVLF，星系性质未完全收敛。

Conclusion: 同时再现多个红移下的多种观测对约束高红移尘埃模型至关重要；ALMA观测可提供独立约束；z>10需要更高分辨率模拟；需谨慎处理反馈方案与尘埃属性之间的简并问题。

Abstract: We present the NINJA suite of cosmological hydrodynamical simulations developed to investigate galaxy formation and evolution at $z \gtrsim 5$ in the era of JWST. Using our fiducial simulation, we explore a range of spectral synthesis prescriptions and dust attenuation models, demonstrating that suitably chosen parameters can reproduce the observed UV luminosity functions (UVLFs) over $5 \leq z \leq 10$. In all cases, the inferred dust-to-metal ratio evolves with redshift, although its normalization at fixed redshift varies by a factor of $\sim 7$, depending on the adopted dust--metallicity scaling and attenuation curve. These model variations introduce substantial scatter in predictions for the $B$-band luminosity function, the H$α$ luminosity function, the UV slope--UV magnitude relation, the stellar mass--Balmer ratio relation, and the relation between stellar and nebular colour excesses. Simultaneously reproducing these observables across multiple redshifts will therefore be essential for constraining dust models at high redshift with forthcoming observations. Observations of galaxies spanning a broad range of stellar masses with the Atacama Large Millimeter/submillimeter Array (ALMA) will provide particularly strong and independent constraints on dust properties. Our fiducial models underpredict the UV luminosity function at $z \geq 10$ relative to current observations, even when adopting a top-heavy IMF and neglecting dust attenuation. We find that galaxy properties are not fully converged at these redshifts in our simulation, indicating that higher-resolution simulations are required to robustly model galaxies at $z > 10$. We further emphasize that degeneracies between feedback prescriptions used in our simulation and dust properties must be carefully addressed when interpreting high-redshift observations and calibrating galaxy formation models.

### [12] [MICONIC: The multiphase circumnuclear region of Centaurus A as seen with JWST/MIRI MRS observations. I. Spectral inventory and properties of the warm molecular disk](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22497)

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (85/100) - 该论文通过JWST MIRI MRS高分辨率光谱，首次定量揭示激波加热而非辐射主导暖H₂气体的冷却与动力学，为用户研究AGN反馈如何通过分子气体输运影响黑洞吸积提供了直接的观测证据和新诊断方法。

TL;DR: 利用JWST/MIRI MRS对半人马座A中心区域的高分辨率光谱观测，研究了分子氢的形态、激发和运动学特征，发现激波加热主导了暖H2气体，抑制了气体冷却和CO发射，同时可能帮助驱动角动量损失为黑洞供能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究近邻射电星系半人马座A内部核周盘的分子氢形态、激发态和运动学，理解AGN反馈如何调节吸积和影响宿主星系。

Method: 利用JWST/MIRI MRS积分场光谱仪对中心170×100 pc²区域进行0.3″-0.7″（5-12 pc）分辨率观测，基于纯转动H2谱线进行激发态拟合，提取温度、柱密度、正-仲氢比等参数，并分析运动学特征。

Result: 首次探测到S(8)线；暖H2形态复杂，中心区域CO弱；低激发H2呈环状结构，20 pc半径空腔与喷流方向对齐；高激发H2呈纤维状结构；运动学呈旋转+S形扭曲，存在向内螺旋的低色散流；暖H2质量(5.6±1.4)×10⁵ M☉，动力学质量5×10⁸ M☉；激波激发由H2/连续谱比、[Ne III]/[Ne II]比和亚平衡正-仲氢比(1.6-2.4)支持；湍流耗散在30 pc外主导加热。

Conclusion: 在半人马座A的100 pc内核中，AGN的供能与反馈紧密耦合：激波激发H2并调节气体温度，阻止气体冷却至100 K以下，从而解释弱的CO发射和缺乏大质量外流；激波可能驱动角动量损失，帮助为核区供能。

Abstract: Supermassive black holes power Active Galactic Nuclei (AGN), injecting energy that regulates accretion and shapes host galaxies. We investigate the morphology, excitation, and kinematics of molecular hydrogen (H2) in the inner circumnuclear disk of Centaurus A, the nearest radio galaxy. We present JWST/MIRI MRS integral-field spectroscopy of the central 170x100 pc2 at 0.3"-0.7" (5-12 pc) resolution, focusing on pure rotational H2 lines. The spectra show strong nuclear continuum and bright H2 emission from S(1) to S(8), including the first S(8) detection in Centaurus A. Optically thin nuclear lines enable maps of temperature, column density, and ortho-to-para ratio from spaxel-level excitation-diagram fitting. Warm H2 shows a complex morphology, dominating the central region where CO emission is weak or undetected. Low-excitation H2 lines trace an inhomogeneous ring with a 20-pc-radius cavity aligned with the jet's near side, suggesting that the jet affects the morphology of the molecular disk. Higher-excitation lines form filamentary structures around the AGN. Kinematics are rotational with an S-shaped distortion, indicating non-circular motions or a warped disk. A coherent, low-dispersion (70 km/s) streamer spirals inward. A power-law temperature distribution yields a warm (100-2000 K) H2 mass of (5.6+/-1.4)e5 Msun and a dynamical mass of 5e8 Msun within 100 pc. Shock excitation is supported by enhanced H2/continuum and H2/PAH ratios, elevated [Ne III]/[Ne II], and sub-equilibrium ortho-to-para ratios (1.6-2.4). Turbulent dissipation can balance H2 cooling and likely dominates heating beyond 30 pc. In the inner 100 pc of Centaurus A, AGN feeding and feedback are linked: shocks excite H2, regulate the gas temperature, and prevent cooling below 100 K, explaining the weak CO emission and lack of a massive outflow. These shocks may drive angular momentum loss and help fuel the nucleus.

### [13] [DREAMS. JWST Spectroscopy of a $z=8.3$ Galaxy with an ALMA Dust Continuum Detection: Early Dust, Very High $T_{\rm dust}$, and a Multi-wavelength [OIII] Ratio Discrepancy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14922)
*Kana Takechi,Masami Ouchi,Kimihiko Nakajima,Tomokazu Kiyota,Yoichi Tamura,Yuichi Harikane,Yurina Nakazato,Tom J. L. C. Bakx,Akio K. Inoue,Hidenobu Yajima,Masato Hagimoto,Yoshiaki Ono,Yi Xu*

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (85/100) - 该论文通过JWST+ALMA联合观测，在z~8星系中同时发现极早期尘埃、超高尘埃温度和宽线AGN，并首次揭示[OIII]光学-红外线比异常，这对理解早期宇宙尘埃形成机制和AGN对ISM影响的观测限制具有直接启发。

TL;DR: 该研究利用JWST/NIRSpec对z=8.312的星系MACS0416-Y1进行观测，发现其存在宽线AGN、中等低金属丰度、极低尘埃质量比，以及异常的[OIII]88μm/[OIII]5007流量比，表明光学和红外发射线示踪了不同区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了表征目前红移最高的ALMA尘埃连续谱探测星系MACS0416-Y1的物理性质，结合JWST、IFU和ALMA多波段数据，特别是理解早期宇宙中AGN活动、尘埃性质和金属丰度的相互作用。

Method: 利用JWST/NIRSpec MSA中分辨率光栅光谱观测，结合存档IFU和ALMA数据，分析Hβ宽线、[OIII]4363发射线、[CII]158μm、尘埃连续谱以及[OIII]88μm/[OIII]5007流量比等多波段谱线特征。

Result: 发现宽线AGN（Hβ线宽~1100 km/s）、金属丰度12+log(O/H)=7.86（0.15太阳丰度）、极低尘埃质量比(log(M_dust/M_gas)~-3.60, log(M_dust/M_metal)~-0.95)、尘埃质量~10^6 M⊙、尘埃温度~91 K，以及非常高的[OIII]88μm/[OIII]5007流量比0.26±0.06。

Conclusion: MACS0416-Y1的金属丰度接近临界值（0.1-0.2太阳丰度），正处于尘埃增长阶段；AGN强紫外辐射导致尘埃温度升高；[OIII]88μm与[OIII]5007示踪不同区域，光学线在尘埃星云中被抑制，因此在JWST+ALMA联合研究中需谨慎解读光学与红外发射线数据。

Abstract: We present a deep DREAMS JWST/NIRSpec MSA medium-grating spectrum of MACS0416-Y1, a galaxy at $z=8.312$ with the highest-redshift ALMA dust continuum detection to date, in order to characterize its properties together with archival IFU and ALMA data. The deep NIRSpec spectrum reveals a broad H$β$ line with a width of $\sim1100$ km s$^{-1}$. We interpret it as a broad-line AGN whose line diagnostics are consistent with AGN activity across its clumpy structure, given the absence of little red dot signatures. MACS0416-Y1 clearly shows [OIII]4363 emission, suggesting a moderately low metallicity of $12+\log(\mathrm{O/H})=7.86^{+0.09}_{-0.08}$ ($0.15~Z_\odot$). The combination of [CII]158$μ$m and dust continuum emission indicates low dust mass ratios of $\log (M_{\rm dust}/M_{\rm gas})=-3.60^{+0.29}_{-0.22}$ and $\log (M_{\rm dust}/M_{\rm metal})=-0.95^{+0.29}_{-0.20}$. Because the metallicity of MACS0416-Y1 is around the critical metallicity of $0.1\textrm{-}0.2~Z_\odot$, the system is expected to undergo dust growth, explaining these low dust mass ratios as well as its small dust mass, $M_{\rm dust}\sim10^6~M_\odot$. The intense UV radiation from the AGN may contribute to a high dust temperature of $T_{\rm dust}\simeq 91^{+62}_{-35}$ K, boosting the dust-continuum emission above the ALMA detection limit despite the small $M_{\rm dust}$ at $z>8$. We find a very high total flux ratio of [OIII]88$μ$m/[OIII]5007 = $0.26 \pm 0.06$ in MACS0416-Y1, above predictions from single ionized nebular models at any electron density. This discrepancy suggests that the [OIII]88$μ$m and [OIII]5007 trace largely distinct regions, with the optical line suppressed in dusty nebulae, and thus requires careful interpretation when combining optical and infrared emission lines in JWST+ALMA studies.

### [14] [Discovery of a Compact Hub-Filament System in G286.21+0.17 with JWST and ALMA: Insights into Protocluster Formation and Competitive Accretion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14693)
*L. K. Dewangan,N. K. Bhadari,Ram K. Yadav,A. K. Maity,O. R. Jadhav,Kee-Tae Kim,Paul F. Goldsmith,A. Saha,Dana Alina,Chang Won Lee,Saurabh Sharma,Tie Liu,Patricio Sanhueza,Tapas Baug,E. Sharma,Fengwei Xu,Ariful Hoque,James O. Chibueze,Dana Makarova,Wenyu Jiao*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (85/100) - 该论文首次联合JWST与ALMA的多波段观测，直接揭示了枢纽-纤维系统中竞争吸积与重力湍流耦合的动力学证据，为你的原恒星/星团形成理论建模提供了高分辨率、多尺度的观测约束。

TL;DR: 利用JWST近红外成像和ALMA H¹³CO⁺(1-0)观测，研究了巨分子云G286.21+0.17中的枢纽-纤维系统，揭示了竞争吸积、重力驱动的湍流以及恒星反馈在星团形成中的重要作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大质量原星团G286.21+0.17的形态结构与动力学演化，理解纤维状吸积和竞争吸积如何在多尺度上调控恒星形成。

Method: 结合JWST近红外成像和ALMA H¹³CO⁺(1-0)分子谱线观测，分析核心径向分布、速度梯度、纤维质量吸积率等特征。

Result: 发现紧凑的枢纽-纤维系统，核心数密度、面密度和封闭质量随半径呈幂律下降，核心直径几乎恒定；纤维质量吸积率在10⁻⁶~10⁻⁴ M☉/yr量级；速度梯度与引力方向未对齐。

Conclusion: G286中的恒星形成受纤维吸积、枢纽区竞争核心增长及恒星反馈共同调节，系统可能已演化至动力学较成熟阶段。

Abstract: We present a multi-wavelength study of the massive protocluster G286.21+0.17 (G286) using \emph{JWST} near-infrared imaging and ALMA H$^{13}$CO$^{+}$(1--0) observations. The \emph{JWST} images uncover a compact ($\sim$0.5 pc) hub-filament system (HFS), comprising a dense central hub connected by at least four converging filaments seen in absorption, along with multiple H$_2$ protostellar jets/outflows. The hub hosts dense core G286c1. The H$^{13}$CO$^{+}$ emission confirms this HFS over [$-$19.2, $-$16.4]~km~s$^{-1}$. The \emph{JWST} images further trace prominent photodissociation regions around the H\,{\sc ii}~region~A, powered by a B-type star. The radial distribution of ALMAGAL 1.38 mm core properties reveals steep power-law slopes toward the hub center. Within the inner hub (r < 8'', $\sim0.1$~pc), the core number density follows $ρ~[\rm pc^{-2}] \propto r^{-2.4\pm0.5}$, the surface density scales as $Σ~[\rm g~cm^{-2}] \propto r^{-1.0\pm0.2}$, and the enclosed core mass varies as $M_{\rm core}~[M_{\odot}] \propto r^{-1.2\pm0.2}$, while core diameters remain approximately constant ($D_{\rm core}~[\rm AU] \propto r^{-0.1\pm0.1}$). These trends, along with filament mass accretion rates of $7\times10^{-6}$--$1.8\times10^{-4}$~$M_\odot$~yr$^{-1}$, support a competitive accretion scenario in which gravitational focusing enhances core growth toward the hub center. Filament linewidths increase from tail/outer-region to head/hub-region, consistent with gravity-driven turbulence. However, the absence of a preferred alignment between velocity gradients and gravitational force directions may indicate a dynamically evolved system. The HFS likely formed through large-scale gas layer interactions and compression by the adjacent H\,{\sc ii} region. Overall, star formation in G286 appears regulated by filamentary accretion, competitive core growth in the hub, and stellar feedback.

TL;DR: 利用ALMA观测蜘蛛网原星系团外围5个尘埃星系中的CO(3-2)，发现它们具有 disturbed 运动学特征，暗示高合并率；气体分数和消耗时标与场星系相似，但最质量星系和X射线AGN的气体分数低于30%，且气体分数和比恒星形成率随距蜘蛛网星系距离增加而下降，支持高红移原星系团中SFR密度-半径关系的反转。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测量z>2原星系团中可用于剧烈恒星形成的冷分子气体性质，是理解大尺度结构形成的关键步骤。

Method: 利用ALMA对蜘蛛网原星系团(z=2.16)核心周围~0.5-4 cMpc范围内的5个尘埃星暴星系进行CO(3-2)观测，测量其分子气体质量和运动学。

Result: 5个星系均显示 disturbed 运动学（非高斯CO线轮廓、不规则空间形态、经典盘模型拟合残差大）；气体分数和消耗时标与场星系相似；最质量星系和X射线AGN气体分数<30%（样品平均49%）；气体分数和sSFR随距蜘蛛网星系距离增加而下降。

Conclusion: 原星系团外围存在升高的并合率；气体供应充足支撑了极高的恒星形成速率；最质量星系和AGN正在失去气体储备；支持原星系团中SFR密度-半径关系的反转。

Abstract: Measuring the properties of cold molecular gas available for intense star formation in galaxy protoclusters at $z>2$ is a crucial step in understanding large scale structure formation. We present ALMA observations of CO(3$-$2) in five dusty star-forming galaxies within $\sim0.5-4$ cMpc of the core of the Spiderweb protocluster at $z=2.16$ to measure the molecular gas mass and kinematics in the most starbursting members of the protocluster. All five galaxies exhibit evidence for disturbed kinematics including non-Gaussian CO line profiles, irregular spatial morphology, and strong residuals when fitting the galaxies with a classical disk model. This could be indicative of an elevated merger rate in the outskirts of the mature Spiderweb protocluster, as all of the galaxies in our sample have multiple companions detected in H$α$. Both the gas fractions and the gas depletion timescales of the galaxies are similar to field relations at cosmic noon, indicative of the fact that their prodigious star formation rates are compensated by similarly high gas masses. The most massive galaxies, as well as all of the galaxies identified as X-ray AGN in previous works, have gas fractions $<30$%, compared to the sample average of 49%, indicating declining availability of gas for star formation. Finally, we find that the gas fractions and specific star formation rates decline with distance from the Spiderweb Galaxy, supporting the reversal of the SFR density--radius relation in high-redshift protoclusters.

### [16] [A quantum theory of the alignment and polarization of very small dust grains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26001)
*Boy Lankhaar*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (85/100) - 这篇论文通过量子对称陀螺模型首次解释了极小尘埃颗粒自旋极化机制，为利用下一代CMB极化实验数据直接探测AME起源和星际磁场提供关键理论支撑。

TL;DR: 本文研究了非常小的星际尘埃颗粒（旋转尘埃/AME）在10-60 GHz频段的异常微波发射（AME）的极化特性，分析了各向异性辐射场如何通过量子力学对称陀螺模型产生可测量的极化信号，并给出了极化分数在最优几何条件下可达百分之一的结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AME的极化既是CMB前景污染源，也是极小尘埃颗粒排列物理的探针，作者希望量化旋转尘埃发射何时能产生可测量的极化，并给出相关的UV/光/IR极化诊断手段。

Method: 发展了一个轴对称极小尘埃颗粒的量子力学对称陀螺模型，用不可约密度矩阵矩表示极化的发射和吸收系数；通过简化的两流形泵浦模型求解各向异性辐射场驱动的颗粒排列，计算了不同偶极构型和颗粒尺寸分布下的（极化）发射和吸收特征。

Result: 各向异性辐射可以产生极化的旋转尘埃发射；在最优几何条件下，发射峰附近的极化分数可达百分之一水平，而更温和的各向异性会降低极化分数；该机制预测的UV/光/IR极化吸收在强辐照环境下可观，而IR振动发射的极化可忽略不计。

Conclusion: 旋转尘埃极化取决于辐射各向异性、偶极几何以及排列泵浦与旋转发射退极化之间的竞争。AME极化与UV/光/IR吸收偏振测量的联合约束可直接检验各向异性辐射场驱动的颗粒排列假说，并有助于约束极化的微波前景。

Abstract: Context. Anomalous microwave emission (AME) is a component of interstellar medium emission peaking at 10-60 GHz. Its polarization is both a CMB foreground and a probe of the alignment physics of very small dust grains. Aims. We quantify when the purely rotational electric-dipole emission from very small interstellar grains (spinning dust/AME) can become measurably polarized, and we quantify related UV/optical/IR polarization diagnostics. Methods. We develop a quantum-mechanical symmetric-top model for an axisymmetric very small grain and express polarized emission and absorption coefficients in terms of irreducible density-matrix moments. Alignment is driven by anisotropic illumination; we solve a simplified two-manifold pumping model and compute (polarized) emission and absorption signatures for different dipole configurations and grain-size distributions. Results. Anisotropic illumination can generate polarized spinning-dust emission; in optimal geometries, polarization fractions near the emission peak reach the percent level, while more modest anisotropies reduce the polarization fraction. The same physics predicts polarized UV/optical/IR absorption that can be appreciable in strongly illuminated environments, whereas IR vibrational emission is predicted to be negligibly polarized. Conclusions. Spinning-dust polarization depends on radiation anisotropy, dipole geometry, and the competition between alignment pumping and depolarization by rotational emission. Joint constraints from AME polarization and UV/optical/IR absorption polarimetry provide a direct test of alignment by anisotropic radiation fields and help bound polarized microwave foregrounds.

### [17] [The ALMA-QUARKS Survey: Multipolar episodic molecular outflow associated with W49N, the most energetic water maser source in the Milky Way](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13671)
*Yunfan Jiao,Tie Liu,Wenyu Jiao,Fengwei Xu,Qilao Gu,Xindi Tang,Xiaofeng Mai,Qiuyi Luo,Siju Zhang,Paul F. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究银河系中最明亮的水脉泽源W49N星暴区的分子外流，旨在深入了解大质量恒星形成过程中的外流机制，探索不同质量恒星形成过程中外流物理机制的普适性。

Result: 在已知的中央双极喷流之外新发现了四个外流瓣，这些外流瓣呈喷流状而非宽开角形态；发现了结链结构（间歇性喷射特征）和S形摆动（进动喷流特征）；获得了更可靠的外流物理参数，确认其为银河系中最具能量的外流之一。

Conclusion: 在极端大质量恒星形成环境中发现通常在小质量原恒星外流中观测到的特征，为外流发射的某些基本物理机制在不同质量恒星形成过程中的保守性提供了有力证据。

Abstract: We present a detailed investigation of a multipolar episodic molecular outflow in the mini-starburst region W49N, which hosts the most luminous water maser in the Galaxy. Using high-resolution ($\sim$0.3 arcsec) Atacama Large Millimeter/submillimeter Array (ALMA) observations of the $\mathrm{^{12}CO}$ emission as part of the ALMA-QUARKS survey, we analyze the morphology and kinematics of the outflow. Our observations reveal four newly identified outflow lobes in addition to the previously known central bipolar jet. These lobes appear more jet-like rather than exhibiting wide opening angles. Based on the $\mathrm{^{12}CO}$ (2--1) and $\mathrm{^{13}CO}$ (2--1) emission, we provide a more reliable estimate of the outflow's physical parameters, confirming it as one of the most energetic outflows in the Galaxy. Notably, these newly discovered lobes exhibit chains of knots, a characteristic signature of episodic ejection. Furthermore, two of the lobes display prominent S-shaped wiggles, suggestive of a precessing jet. The discovery of these features -- commonly observed in outflows from low-mass protostars -- in such an extreme massive star-forming environment provides compelling evidence that some underlying physical mechanisms for launching outflows are conserved across a wide range of stellar masses.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用ALMA新Band 2接收器完成ALMA全（亚）毫米波频率覆盖，通过宽频谱覆盖（76-111 GHz）同时获取大量分子和原子发射线，研究高红移星系SPT 0027的分子气体特性，并展示ALMA Band 2在宇宙正午及更远红移（z~1-6）进行稳健光谱红移测量的独特能力。

Method: 使用ALMA Band 2接收器（67-116 GHz）对红移z=3.44的强引力透镜亚毫米星系SPT 0027进行分子谱线巡测，观测频段为76-111 GHz，同时探测多种分子和原子发射线，并结合高分辨率Band 7连续谱成像分析星系形态。

Result: 首次探测到CO(3-2)和HNC(4-3)线，同时观测到先前已知的CO(4-3)、[CI]、HCN(5-4)、HCO⁺(5-4)和HNC(5-4)线；CO谱线能量分布和[CI]/CO线比表明存在高度激发、致密的分子气体和强远紫外辐射场；致密气体比例估计为17±9%；高分辨率成像显示透镜形态呈团块状，星形成团块贡献总发射的30-50%。

Conclusion: ALMA Band 2凭借其宽频覆盖和多个CO线可观测性，成为在宇宙正午及更远红移（z~1-6）进行稳健光谱红移测量的理想工具，这一能力将通过宽带灵敏度升级进一步增强。

Abstract: I present the first molecular line survey of the strongly lensed submillimetre galaxy SPT 0027 ($z = 3.44$) using the new Atacama Large Millimeter/submillimeter Array (ALMA) Band~2 receivers (67 - 116 GHz), whose commissioning completes ALMA's full (sub-)millimetre frequency coverage. The broad spectral coverage from 76 to 111 GHz of the observations simultaneously accesses a large suite of molecular and atomic emission lines. I report the novel detections of the hitherto inaccessible CO (3-2) and HNC (4-3) lines, as well as detections of previously-observed CO (4-3) transitions, the neutral carbon line [CI], HCN (5-4), HCO$^{+}$ (5-4), and HNC (5-4), with fluxes in line with previous observations. The CO spectral line energy distribution and [CI]/CO line ratios indicate highly excited, dense molecular gas with a strong far-ultraviolet radiation field. The dense gas fraction is estimated at $17 \pm 9$ per cent, consistent with other dusty star-forming galaxies selected from wide-area surveys. High-resolution Band 7 continuum imaging reveals a clumpy lensed morphology, with star-forming clumps contributing 30-50 per cent of the total emission. With multiple CO lines accessible across a wide redshift range, ALMA Band 2 is uniquely positioned as the premier tool for robust spectroscopic redshifts at Cosmic Noon and beyond ($z \sim 1$-$6$), a capability that will be further enhanced by the Wideband Sensitivity Upgrade's full-band coverage in fewer tunings.

</details>

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (85/100) - 通过排除Gaia干扰项找到低红移强透镜，这种搜索策略直接提升了强透镜统计样本的完备性，可用于精确约束低红移星系的质量分布和暗物质子结构。

TL;DR: 在Euclid Quick Release 1数据中发现了72个新的星系-星系强引力透镜候选体，通过改进的搜索方法找到了之前因排除Gaia目录对象而遗漏的明亮低红移透镜，使高置信度候选体总数达到38个。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 之前基于机器学习模型的预筛选排除了Gaia目录中的对象，导致遗漏了许多明亮且红移较低的强引力透镜系统。本研究旨在通过改进搜索方法，发现这些被遗漏的透镜候选体，完善Euclid巡天中的强透镜样本。

Method: 采用两种独立搜索方法：1）基于机器学习模型筛选后专家目视检查；2）直接对未包含在初始机器学习选择中的对象进行专家目视检查。通过半自动透镜建模对候选体进行确认。

Result: 共发现72个新的强透镜候选体，其中38个为"A级"（高置信度），34个为"B级"（可能）。半自动建模确认了至少41个系统。这些透镜包括：多个侧向盘状透镜、弧线靠近透镜中心的源、"红色源"、以及一个透镜星系合并的侧向盘状星系。中位红移比SLDE A样本低约0.3。

Conclusion: 改进的搜索方法成功发现了之前遗漏的明亮低红移强透镜，将Euclid宽视场巡天中预期的高置信度候选体数量提升至12万个。这些新增样本丰富了强透镜的多样性，为宇宙学和星系形成研究提供了宝贵资源。

Abstract: We present 72 additional galaxy-galaxy strong lenses that complement the sample discovered in the Euclid Quick Release 1 data (63.1 deg^2) of the Strong Lens Discovery Engine (SLDE) papers A-E. It is shown that previous pre-selection of potential lenses, which excluded objects from the Gaia catalogue, led to missing several bright and low-redshift strong lenses, adding more than 10% new strong lens candidates compared to the previous search. In total, the catalogue includes 38 "grade A" (confident) and 34 "grade B" (probable) candidates. These lenses are identified through a combination of two independent searches for bright nearby objects: one based on machine-learning models followed by expert visual inspection, and the other based solely on expert visual inspection, targeting objects not included in the initial machine-learning selection (a limitation identified only after extensive visual inspection). With these additional strong lens candidates, we augment the expected number of high-confidence candidates in the Euclid Wide Survey from previous forecasts to 120000. Detailed semi-automated lens modelling confirms at least 41 systems out of 72, a fraction consistent with that found in SLDE A (315 out of 488). These include: multiple edge-on disc lenses; sources with arcs near the lens centre; "red sources"; and an edge-on disk galaxy lensing a galaxy merger, producing two sets of lensed features, an Einstein ring and a doubly imaged component. The median redshift of these systems is $Δ$ z ~ 0.3 lower than that of the SLDE A sample.

### [20] [Estimation of the magnetic field strength from ALMA dust polarization in the protocluster G327.29](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23747)
*A. Koley,P. Sanhueza,A. M. Stutz,P. Saha,F. A. Olguin,A. Ginsburg,N. Sandoval-Garrido,N. Castro-Toledo*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (85/100) - 该论文通过ALMA高分辨率尘埃极化观测直接测量了原星团G327.29的磁场形态，并发现磁场主导湍流，这对理解大质量恒星形成中的动力学平衡机制具有方法学上的示范价值，尤其适合关注分子云碎裂和磁流体动力学演化的研究者。

TL;DR: 利用ALMA高分辨率观测G327.29大质量恒星形成区的磁场形态，发现磁场比湍流对恒星形成过程更具动力学重要性


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁场和湍流在分子云演化和恒星形成中起关键作用，但其具体作用机制仍不清楚。研究旨在通过高分辨率观测理解磁场、湍流和重力在大质量恒星形成中的相对重要性

Method: 使用ALMA 12米望远镜对G327.29区域进行高分辨率平面天空磁场观测，采用角弥散函数方法计算总磁场强度，分析磁场形态、湍流与磁场能量比以及维里参数

Result: 观测到复杂的磁场形态，磁场方向在-90到+90度范围内均匀分布；在密度6.8×10^5 cm^-3和1.1×10^6 cm^-3区域测得总磁场强度分别为1.4±0.7 mG和2.0±0.8 mG；湍流与磁场能量比约0.25，表明磁场比湍流更具动力学重要性；维里参数显示区域可能受重力束缚或未束缚

Conclusion: 磁场在大质量恒星形成区G327.29中比湍流更具动力学重要性，湍流和磁场对核心动力学的相对影响取决于总磁场强度随气体密度的变化关系

Abstract: Magnetic fields and turbulence may play a crucial role in the evolution of molecular clouds and ultimately in the formation of dense cores and stars. Despite being studied in many molecular clouds, the exact role of magnetic fields and turbulence in star formation is still poorly understood. Here, we report the high resolution plane of sky magnetic field (B_pos) morphology toward the high mass star forming region G327.29, obtained with the 12-meter of the Atacama Large Millimeter/sub-millimeter Array (ALMA) telescope. From our analysis, we obtain a complex B_pos morphology where the magnetic field orientation is uniformly distributed across the entire range from -90 to +90 deg. The observed area is composed of one filament and one dense central clump, which harbor multiple dense cores. The total magnetic field strengths (B_tot) in these regions are 1.4 \pm 0.7 mG and 2.0 \pm 0.8 mG at a number density (n) of 6.8 \pm 1.5 x 10^5 and 1.1 \pm 0.3 x 10^6 cm^-3 , derived from the angular dispersion function (ADF) method. The virial parameters (α vir )in these regions are 7.7 \pm 7.1 and 0.7 \pm 0.6, suggesting that the regions may be gravitationally bound or unbound after accounting for the errors. Moreover, the ratio of turbulent to magnetic energy (~ 0.25) indicates that the magnetic field is dynamically more important than turbulence. The relative influence of turbulence and magnetic fields on core dynamics appears to depend on how the B_tot scales with gas density (\r{ho}) in the densest regions. In summary, this work presents a comprehensive analysis of the relative roles of magnetic fields, turbulence, and gravity in regulating high-mass star formation in G327.29, enabled by high-resolution ALMA observations.

</details>


### [21] [JOYS: Linking the molecular ice and gas-phase composition towards the high-mass hot core IRAS 18089-1732](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22007)
*C. Gieser,W. R. M. Rocha,Y. Chen,K. Slavicinska,E. F. van Dishoeck,P. Nazari,N. G. C. Brunken,L. Francis,H. Beuther,S. Reyes-Reyes,A. Caratti o Garatti,P. D. Klaassen,J. M. Vorster,M. G. Navarro*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (85/100) - 该论文通过JWST与ALMA的多波段协同观测，直接对比了冰相与气相分子的丰度差异，为揭示高质星形成区分子云化学演化路径提供了关键的观测约束，这种跨相位关联分析的方法可推广至你的相关研究中。

TL;DR: JWST和ALMA观测揭示年轻大质量热核IRAS 18089-1732中冰相和气相分子的丰度分布，发现部分分子在两相中丰度相似，部分存在显著差异，暗示不同的形成路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在JWST发射前，对星际介质中除主要成分外的冰相分子探测存在灵敏度、角分辨率和光谱分辨率不足的挑战。本研究旨在利用JWST的高灵敏度观测，结合ALMA的气相数据，全面表征年轻大质量热核区域中冰相和气相分子的丰度分布。

Method: 使用JWST在5-28微米波段的光谱数据推导冰相分子柱密度，包括H2O、SO2、OCN-、CH4等12种分子；同时利用ALMA在3毫米波段的分子谱线观测推导38种气相分子（包括O、N、S、Si等元素物种及其同位素）的柱密度。

Result: 发现C2H5OH、CH3OH和CH3OCH3在冰相和气相中的丰度（相对于C2H5OH或CH3OH）相当；SO2和CH3COCH3在气相中丰度更高，暗示额外的气相形成路径；CH3CHO在冰相中的丰度比气相高一个数量级。IRAS 18089热核的冰丰度（相对于H2O冰）与先前研究的银河系低质量和高质量原恒星相似，OCN-、CH3OH和CH3CHO冰的丰度可能随银心距增加而降低。

Conclusion: JWST的高灵敏度观测首次实现了对年轻大质量热核区域中多种冰相分子的详细探测，结合ALMA的气相数据，揭示了冰相和气相分子丰度的相似性和差异性，为理解星际介质中分子的形成和演化机制提供了重要线索。

Abstract: Context. The formation and destruction of molecules in the interstellar medium is a complex interplay between gas-phase reactions as well as processes on grain surfaces and within icy mantles. For many decades, the gas-phase composition of the cold material towards star-forming regions could be well characterized using (sub)mm facilities. Prior to the launch of the James Webb Space Telescope (JWST), ice species other than the main constituents (H2O, CO, CO2, NH3, CH4, CH3OH) were challenging to detect due to insufficient sensitivity as well as angular and/or spectral resolution. Aims. We determine molecular ice and gas-phase column densities towards the young and embedded high-mass hot core IRAS 18089-1732 within a region of 5000 au. Methods. We use spectroscopic data from 5-28 micron obtained with JWST to derive ice column densities of H2O, SO2, OCN-, CH4, HCOO-, HCOOH, CH3CHO, CH3COOH, C2H5OH, CH3OCH3, and CH3COCH3. Gas-phase column densities of a total of 38 molecules, including, O-, N-, S-, and Si-bearing species as well as less abundant isotopologues, are inferred from sensitive molecular line observations taken with the Atacama Large Millimeter/submillimeter Array (ALMA) at 3 mm wavelengths. Results. We find comparable abundances (relative to C2H5OH or CH3OH) in both phases for C2H5OH, CH3OH, and CH3OCH3. The abundances of SO2 and CH3COCH3 are higher in the gas-phase suggesting additional gas-phase formation routes. The abundance of CH3CHO is one order of magnitude higher in the ices compared to the gas-phase. The ice abundances (relative to H2O ice) towards the IRAS 18089 hot core are similar to previously studied Galactic low- and high-mass protostars. There are hints of a decreasing abundance with Galactocentric distance for OCN-, CH3OH, and CH3CHO ice. (abridged)

</details>


### [22] [The ionised interstellar medium of DSFGs revealed by JWST/NIRSpec and ALMA: Super-solar metallicity, low ionisation parameters and, typical electron densities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.18558)
*Steven Gillman,Kei Ito,Francesco Valentino,Gabe Brammer,Pablo Araya Araya,Georgios Magdis,Ugnė Dudzevičiūtė,Aswin P. Vijayan,Minju Lee,Bitten Gullberg,Daniel Ceverino,Andreas L. Faisst,Seiji Fujimoto,Thomas R. Greve,Rashmi Gottumukkala,Chandana Hegde,Michaela Hirschmann,Shuowen Jin,Christian Kragh Jespersen,Takumi Kakimoto,Mariko Kubo,Peter Laursen,Masato Onodera,Antonio Pensabene,Francesca Rizzo,John R. Weaver,Po-Feng Wu*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (85/100) - 该论文利用JWST/NIRSpec与ALMA联合观测，揭示了高红移星系超太阳金属丰度与低电离参数，对你的星际介质化学演化和尘埃-金属平衡关系研究具有直接观测约束价值。

TL;DR: JWST/NIRSpec观测48个高红移ALMA星系，发现这些远红外明亮星系是质量大、化学演化成熟的系统，偏离了标准尘埃-金属平衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高红移、尘埃遮蔽的恒星形成星系的性质，特别是它们的金属丰度、电子密度和电离参数，以了解这些系统的星际介质特征和演化状态。

Method: 使用JWST/NIRSpec获取近红外光谱(2-4μm)，结合ALMA探测，对48个高红移(z=2.53)星系进行多波段SED分析，测量金属丰度([NII]/Hα)、电子密度([SII]双线比)和电离参数([OII]/Hβ)。

Result: 样本中位恒星质量log(M*/M⊙)=10.8±0.1，尘埃质量log(Md/M⊙)=8.7±0.1；金属丰度12+log(O/H)=8.71±0.02，最明亮的FIR星系偏离基本金属丰度关系0.15±0.03dex；电子密度log(ne/cm³)=2.53±0.07；电离参数log(U)=-2.84±0.06；40%星系显示AGN活动迹象。

Conclusion: 远红外明亮星系是质量大、化学演化成熟的系统，偏离了在较少尘埃遮蔽星系中观察到的标准尘埃和金属产生平衡，突显了JWST和ALMA协同研究的重要性。

Abstract: We present a detailed study of near-infrared (2-4$\rm μ$m) JWST/NIRSpec spectra of 48 high-redshift ($z=2.53^{+1.32}_{-0.70}$) galaxies detected with ALMA at $>3σ$. From a multi-wavelength SED analysis we establish the sample has a a median stellar mass of $\rm\log_{10}(M_\ast/M_\odot)=10.8\pm0.1$ and dust mass of $\rm\log_{10}(M_{\rm d}/M_\odot)=8.7\pm0.1$, covering a broad range of far-infrared luminosity $\rm (\log_{10}(L_{FIR}/L_\odot)=10.9-12.7)$. The majority of sources show no signs of AGN activity, with 40% having either X-ray counterparts $(\rm L_{Xc}>10^{42}erg/s)$, elevated optical line ratios, or broad (FWHM>800 km/s) H$α$ profiles, although we note this is a lower limit due to the stochastic placement of NIRSpec slits. We establish the sample has a median gas-phase metallicity of $12+\log({\rm O/H})=8.71\pm0.02$, as derived from the [NII]/H$α$ ratio, with the most FIR-luminous galaxies ($\rm\log_{10}(L_{\rm FIR}/L_\odot)>12$) falling $0.15\pm0.03$dex above the fundamental metallicity relation. From the [SII] emission-line doublet ratio, we measure a median electron density of $\log_{10}(n_{\rm e}/{\rm cm}^{-3})=2.53\pm0.07$ consistent with less-massive, star-forming, galaxies at the same epoch. For nine galaxies with [OII] and H$β$ detections (median $\rm\log_{10}(L_{\rm FIR}/L_\odot)=11.81\pm0.15$), we derive a median observed (dust-uncorrected) ionisation parameter of $\rm\log_{10}(U)=-2.84\pm0.06$. Our results indicate that luminous far-infrared galaxies are massive, chemically evolved systems that appear to deviate from the standard dust and metal production equilibrium observed in less obscured galaxies. This study demonstrates the synergy of JWST and ALMA in unveiling the nature of DSFGs, and highlights the need for a NIRSpec survey of uniformly selected, massive, dust-obscured, galaxies to fully characterise their interstellar medium.

</details>


### [23] [The ALMA-QUARKS Survey: Discovery of Dusty Fibrils inside Massive Star-forming Clumps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.11617)
*Yan-Kun Zhang,Tie Liu,Wenyu Jiao,Pak-Shing Li,Jia Zeng,Chao Zhang,Pablo García,Mika Juvela,Guido Garay,Amelia M. Stutz,Sami Dib,Dezhao Meng,Jian-Cheng Feng,Dongting Yang,Fengwei Xu,Anandmayee Tej,Enrique Vázquez-Semadeni,Gilberto C. Gómez,Yong Zhang,Xindi Tang,Paul F. Goldsmith,Kee-Tae Kim,James O. Chibueze,Zhiyuan Ren,Patricio Sanhueza,Aiyuan Yang,Jihye Hwang,Shanghuo Li,Tapas Baug,Shivani Gupta,Swagat R. Das,Gang Wu,Jianjun Zhou,Chang Won Lee,Lokesh Dewangan,Prasanta Gorai,Tianning Lyu,Lei Zhu*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (85/100) - 该论文通过ALMA高分辨率观测揭示了比赫歇尔纤维细10倍的超细纤维结构及其密度分布，直接挑战了现有恒星形成初始条件的尺度层级模型，对理解大质量恒星形成中纤维的分裂与坍缩机制具有关键启发。

TL;DR: ALMA-QUARKS巡天在121个大质量恒星形成团块中发现了323个超细尘埃纤维结构，其典型宽度约0.01 pc，比赫歇尔望远镜发现的纤维细10倍，密度更高（N_H2=10^23-10^24 cm^-2），质量与长度关系遵循M∝L^2。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究大质量恒星形成团块中的细尺度纤维结构，探索不同银河系环境中的纤维性质，理解纤维结构在恒星形成中的关键作用。

Method: 使用ALMA-QUARKS巡天的1.3 mm连续谱数据（线性分辨率约900 AU），通过FilFinder软件识别纤维结构，用RadFil软件测量纤维宽度，分析质量与长度关系。

Result: 在121个大质量恒星形成团块中发现323个超细纤维，典型宽度约0.01 pc，比赫歇尔发现的纤维细10倍；质量与长度关系遵循M∝L^2；密度显著更高（N_H2=10^23-10^24 cm^-2）。

Conclusion: 这项工作提供了大质量团块中超细纤维的大样本，强调了纤维结构在不同物理尺度恒星形成中的关键作用，与先前在邻近分子云中发现的0.1 pc宽纤维和速度相干纤维的研究相呼应。

Abstract: We report the discovery of more than 323 superfine dusty filamentary structures (fibrils) inside 121 massive star forming clumps that are located in widely different Galactic environments (Galactocentric distances of $\sim$0.5-12.7 kpc). These fibrils are identified from the 1.3~mm continuum emission in the ALMA-QUARKS survey, which has a linear resolution of $\sim900$ AU for a source at $\sim$3 kpc, using the \textit{FilFinder} software. Using \textit{RadFil} software, we find that the typical width of these fibrils is $\sim$0.01 pc, which is about ten times narrower than that of dusty filaments in nearby clouds identified by the \textit{Herschel} Space Observatory. The mass ($M$) versus length ($L$) relation for these fibrils follows $M\propto L^{2}$, similar to that of Galactic filaments identified in space (e.g., \textit{Herschel}) and ground-based single-dish (e.g., \textit{APEX}) surveys. However, these fibrils are significantly denser ($\mathrm{N_{H_2} = 10^{23}-10^{24}\ cm^{-2}}$) than the filaments found in previous \textit{Herschel} surveys ($\mathrm{N_{H_2} = 10^{20}-10^{23}\ cm^{-2}}$). This work contributes a large sample of superfine fibrils in massive clumps, following the identification of large 0.1-pc wide filaments and associated internal velocity coherent fibers in nearby molecular clouds, further emphasizing the crucial role played by filamentary structures in star formation at various physical scales.

### [24] [MAGAZ3NE: Dust Deficiency in Ultramassive Quiescent Galaxies at $3<z<4$ with ALMA Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22844)
*Wenjun Chang,Gillian Wilson,Ben Forrest,Ian McConachie,Allison Noble,Adam Muzzin,Danilo Marchesini,Michael C. Cooper,Tracy Webb,Gabriela Canalizo,Percy L. Gomez,Yongda Zhu,Adit Edward,Han Lei,Aurélien Henry,Stephanie M. Urbano Stawinski,Marie E. Wisz*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (85/100) - 该论文通过ALMA亚毫米波观测直接排除了尘埃遮蔽恒星形成的可能，对研究早期宇宙中超大质量星系熄灭机制和尘埃演化模型提供了关键观测约束。

TL;DR: 利用ALMA Band 7观测确认了5个z>3的超大质量星系中，4个是真正的静止星系，具有极低的尘埃含量，排除了尘埃遮蔽的恒星形成可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在z>3时区分真正的静止星系和尘埃遮蔽的恒星形成星系是一个主要挑战，因为两者都具有相似的紫外到近红外颜色。需要更直接的观测方法来确认这些系统的真实性质。

Method: 使用ALMA Band 7对MAGAZ3NE巡天中5个光谱确认的z>3超大质量星系进行尘埃连续谱观测，并结合光谱能量分布分析来区分星系性质。

Result: 5个星系中只有1个有微弱的870微米尘埃连续谱探测，其余4个在3σ深度下未探测到。这些星系确实处于静止状态，位于恒星形成主序线下超过1个数量级，排除了遮蔽恒星形成的可能性。其中3个星系具有极低的尘埃质量比(Mdust/M⋆ ≲ 10⁻⁴)。

Conclusion: 这是目前已知在3<z<4范围内最大质量且尘埃极少的静止星系，为早期宇宙中快速尘埃移除和淬灭过程提供了重要观测约束。未来需要分子谱线观测来直接测量气体含量。

Abstract: A major challenge in identifying massive quiescent galaxies at $z>3$ is distinguishing truly passive systems from dust-obscured star-forming galaxies, as both populations exhibit similar red ultraviolet (UV)-to-near-infrared (NIR) colors. In this work, we present ALMA Band 7 dust-continuum observations of five ultramassive galaxies (UMGs; $\log (M_\star / M_\odot) > 11$) spectroscopically confirmed at $z_{\rm spec} > 3$ from the MAGAZ3NE survey. Our results reveal that only one galaxy shows a faint 870 \um\ dust continuum detection, while the remaining four UMGs are undetected down to the $3σ$ depth . By incorporating ALMA constraints into the spectral energy distribution analysis, we confirm that these UV-NIR-selected systems are truly quiescent UMGs, lying more than one dex below the star-forming main sequence with $\mathrm{\log (sSFR/Gyr^{-1}) < -1}$, thereby ruling out the possibility of obscured star formation. We then estimate dust masses using both spectral energy distribution modeling and modified blackbody fitting, with consistent results between the two methods. We find that three UMGs have evolved into extremely dust-poor quiescent galaxies, with $M_{\mathrm{dust}}/M_\star \lesssim 10^{-4}$, while the ALMA-detected galaxy has a comparatively higher dust reservoir with $M_{\mathrm{dust}}/M_\star \sim 10^{-3}$. Our results present the most massive and extremely dust-poor spectroscopically confirmed quiescent galaxies known at $3 < z < 4$, providing valuable observational constraints on rapid dust removal and quenching processes in the early universe. Future molecular line observations will be essential to directly measure the gas content and verify the efficiency of the depletion process.

### [25] [Breathless BEARS: [O$_{\rm \,III}$] 88$μ$m Emission of Dusty Star-Forming Galaxies at $z = 3-4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09780)
*T. J. L. C. Bakx,Hiddo S. B. Algera,Prachi Prajapati,George Bendo,Stefano Berta,Laura Bonavera,Pierre Cox,Joaquin González-Nuevo,Masato Hagimoto,Kevin Harrington,Matthew Lehnert,Stephen Serjeant,Pasquale Temi,Paul van der Werf,Chentao Yang,Gianfranco De Zotti*

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (85/100) - 该论文通过ACA对高红移尘埃恒星形成星系[OIII]88μm发射的精确测量，揭示了其与本地星系迥异的星族和尘埃环境，为研究早期宇宙星系演化提供了关键的观测约束。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高红移尘埃恒星形成星系(DSFGs)的[OIII]88μm发射特性，填补低红移空间观测和高红移地面研究之间的空白，理解这类过渡性星系系统的物理性质。

Method: 使用Atacama Compact Array(ACA)的Band 9和10对4个Herschel选出的高红移尘埃恒星形成星系(z=2.9-4)进行[OIII]88μm观测，部分目标还获得了[CII]发射的辅助数据。

Result: 所有4个目标都检测到>3σ的[OIII]发射，线光度比(L[OIII]/LIR = 10^{-4.2}到10^{-3})与本地旋涡星系相似，但比本地矮星系和高红移Lyman-break星系低一个数量级。L[OIII]/L[CII]比值为0.3-0.9。

Abstract: We present [O$_{\rm \,III}$] 88$μ$m observations towards four ${\it Herschel}$-selected dusty star-forming galaxies (DSFGs; log$_{10}$ $μ$L$_{\rm IR}$/L$_{\odot}$ = 13.5 - 14 at $z = 2.9 - 4$) using the Atacama Compact Array (ACA) in Bands 9 and 10. We detect [O$_{\rm \,III}$] emission in all four targets at >3$σ$, finding line luminosity ratios ($L_{\rm [O_{\rm \,III}]}$ / L$_{\rm IR}$ = 10$^{-4.2}$ to 10$^{-3}$) similar to local spiral galaxies, and an order of magnitude lower when compared with local dwarf galaxies as well as high-redshift Lyman-break galaxies. Using the short-wavelength capabilities of the ACA, these observations bridge the populations of galaxies with [O$_{\rm \,III}$] emission at low redshift from space missions and at high redshift from ground-based studies. The difference in [O$_{\rm \,III}$] emission between these DSFGs and other high-redshift galaxies reflects their more evolved stellar populations (> 10 Myr), larger dust reservoirs (M$_{\rm dust}$ $\sim$ 10$^{9 - 11}$ M$_{\odot}$), metal-rich interstellar medium ($Z \sim 0.5 - 2$ Z$_{\odot}$), and likely weaker ionization radiation fields. Ancillary [C$_{\rm \,II}$] emission on two targets provide $L_{[{\rm O}_{\rm \,III}]} / L_{[{\rm C}_{\rm \,II}]}$ ratios at 0.3 - 0.9, suggesting that ionized gas represents a smaller fraction of the total gas reservoir in DSFGs, consistent with theoretical models of DSFGs as transitional systems between gas-rich, turbulent disks and more evolved, gas-poor galaxies. Expanding samples of DSFGs with [O$_{\rm \,III}$] emission will be key to place this heterogeneous, poorly-understood galactic phase in its astrophysical context.

### [26] [Fast rotations in galaxies at cosmic noon indicate central concentration of stars, dark matter or massive black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.03338)
*Fernanda Roman-Oliveira,Francesca Rizzo,Filippo Fraternali*

TL;DR: 该研究结合ALMA和JWST观测数据，分析三个高红移盘状星系的旋转曲线，发现动力学模型在星系中心区域低估了旋转速度，表明存在中心质量缺失或暗物质分布异常。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高红移星系（z>0.5）的旋转曲线分析一直面临挑战，缺乏高分辨率运动学数据、准确追踪恒星表面密度的测光数据以及空间分辨的亚毫米观测来追踪冷气体分布。本研究旨在利用ALMA和JWST的先进观测能力，研究高红移盘状星系的动力学特性并约束其暗物质晕。

Method: 从ALPAKA样本中选取三个星系，结合ALMA的高分辨率冷气体观测和JWST的静止近红外成像数据。这些星系最初仅基于ALMA观测被分类为规则旋转盘。通过构建动力学模型来模拟星系的旋转曲线，并与观测数据进行比较。

Result: JWST观测显示这些星系是延伸的对称恒星盘，带有旋臂结构。动力学模型能够很好地再现星系外围区域的旋转，但系统性地低估了中心区域的旋转速度，揭示了相对于观测数据的中心质量缺失。

Conclusion: 观测与模型之间的差异表明：1）由于恒星质量-光比变化或尘埃消光导致核球质量被低估；2）存在超大质量黑洞；3）偏离标准暗物质晕分布，包括增强的中心浓度。这些发现对高红移星系的暗物质分布和中心质量构成提出了重要问题。

Abstract: The rotation curves of regularly rotating disc galaxies are a unique probe of the gravitational potential and dark matter distribution. Until recently, matter decomposition of rotation curves at $z>0.5$ was challenging, not only due to the lack of high resolution kinematic data but also of both suitable photometry to accurately trace the stellar surface density and spatially-resolved sub-mm observations to trace the cold gas distribution. In this paper, we analyse three galaxies from the Archival Large Program to Advance Kinematic Analysis (ALPAKA) sample, combining highly resolved cold gas observations from ALMA with rest-frame near-infrared imaging from JWST to investigate their dynamical properties and constrain their dark matter halos. The galaxies, initially classified as regularly rotating discs based on ALMA observations alone, appear in JWST as extended and symmetric stellar discs with spiral arms. Our dynamical models reproduce the rotation of the discs in the outer parts well, but they systematically underpredict the inner rotation velocities, revealing a deficit of central mass relative to the data. This discrepancy indicates either an underestimation of the bulge masses due to variations in the stellar mass-to-light ratio or dust attenuation or the presence of overmassive black holes. Alternatively, it may suggest departures from standard dark-matter halo profiles, including enhanced central concentrations.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Determining the physical properties of galaxies during the first billion years after the big bang is key to understanding both early galaxy evolution and how galaxies contributed to the epoch of reionization. We present deep ALMA observations of the redshifted [OIII] 88um line for the gravitationally lensed ($μ= 11.4\pm1.9$) galaxy A383-5.1 (z=6.027) that has previously been detected in [CII] 158um. Recent James Webb Space Telescope (JWST) imaging identified this sub-L* galaxy as a ''Little Red Dot'' (LRD). With a line luminosity of $L_{\rm [OIII]} = (1.29\pm0.24)\times10^8$ L$_\odot$ (corrected for lensing magnification) A383-5.1 is one of the faintest galaxies with combined [CII] and [OIII] detections. The ALMA data reveal no dust continuum emission, consistent with previous observations. The high line luminosity ratio of [OIII]/[CII] $\sim 14\pm5$ is consistent with A383-5.1 being low-metallicity and dust-poor. The non-detection of dust continuum in bands 6 and 8 is consistent with the high [OIII]/[CII] ratio and suggests a presence of a strong ultraviolet radiation field, which would be less affect by dust attenuation, implying that galaxies of this type could contribute significantly to the ionization of the intergalactic medium. The presence of strong ionizing field could provide an important piece of information for understanding the nature of LRDs and their role in cosmic reionization.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高红移尘埃星系的分子气体性质及其与恒星形成的关系尚不明确，缺乏高分辨率多波段协同观测来揭示其内部物理机制。

Method: 利用ALMA对三个ALESS巡天中的z~3亚毫米星系进行CO(5-4)和CO(4-3)高分辨率成像，结合ALMA 870μm连续谱和JWST多波段数据，进行运动学建模和kpc尺度标度关系分析。

Result: 1) 两个源处于同一红移且可能相互作用；2) 分子气体分布比尘埃辐射更延展，与近红外恒星辐射尺度相当；3) 运动学符合旋转盘模型（V_max/σ=5±1和6±1）；4) kpc尺度标度关系偏离无湍流理论预测，但与引力湍流模型一致。

Conclusion: 湍流在高红移星系中调控恒星形成中起核心作用。

Abstract: We present ALMA high-resolution ($\sim$0.25$^{\prime\prime}$/2 kpc) CO(5-4) and CO(4-3) observations of three $z\sim 3$ submillimetre-selected dusty galaxies from the ALESS survey. These data complement existing [sub]-kpc scale ALMA 870$μ$m continuum imaging and JWST NIRCam and MIRI imaging from the ALESS-JWST program, allowing us to trace the molecular gas, dust-obscured star formation, and stellar populations on similar spatial scales. We spectroscopically confirm that two of the sources lie at the same redshift and are likely interacting. We find that the molecular-gas distribution broadly follows the dusty star-forming structures seen in the 870$μ$m dust continuum imaging, but that the gas reservoirs are significantly more extended than the dust emission with a spatial extent comparable to the rest-frame near-infrared stellar emission. By modeling the kinematics for the two highest signal-to-noise sources, we find that the galaxies are well-fit by rotating disc models with high ratios of ordered to random motion ($V_{\rm{max}}/\overlineσ=5\pm1$ and $6\pm1$), although smaller-scale kinematic deviations cannot be ruled out at the current sensitivity and spatial resolution. Finally, utilizing the high-resolution 870$μ$m dust continuum and CO data, we investigate star-formation scaling relations on kpc-scales in these high-redshift galaxies. Assuming a constant CO-to-H$_{2}$ conversion factor and excitation ratio, we find that the data are offset from theoretical star-formation relation predictions that do not take turbulence into account, but consistent with gravo-turbulent models, thereby suggesting that turbulence plays a central role in regulating star formation at high redshift.

</details>


### [29] [ALMA High-resolution Observation of the HH46/47 Outflow/disk/envelope System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08607)
*Heyi Zhang,Yichen Zhang,Héctor G. Arce,Diego Mardones,Sylvie Cabrit,Michael M. Dunham,Stella S. R. Offner,Hsien Shang*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (82/100) - 该论文的ALMA高分辨率观测揭示了双星相互作用对旋转包层动力学的具体影响，为解析多星系统形成和恒星反馈提供了可直接借鉴的运动学建模范例。

TL;DR: 利用ALMA高分辨率观测揭示了HH 46/47分子外流及其包层-盘系统的精细结构，包括双星相互作用、旋转内落包层动力学以及外壳层的膨胀运动学特征。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通过亚毫米波高分辨率观测，解析HH 46/47系统中包层-盘结构、双星相互作用以及分子外流的详细动力学过程，以理解恒星形成中的物质传输和反馈机制。

Method: 使用ALMA 1.3 mm连续谱和多种分子谱线（C18O、SO、H2CO、CH3OH、12CO、13CO）观测，结合JWST NIRCam图像，进行光学深度校正和模型无关的动力学分析。

Result: 发现了围绕双星系统的环双星盘中的子结构和两个旋臂状特征；C18O示踪扩展包层，SO示踪内包层，H2CO和CH3OH示踪离心势垒附近的致密快速旋转结构；旋转内落模型拟合得到~30 au的盘半径和0.3 Msun的原恒星；发现外流中多个壳层结构，其中红移壳层呈径向膨胀而非表面流动；横向速度梯度若解释为旋转则导致非物理的磁力臂参数，更支持夹带机制。

Conclusion: HH 46/47系统呈现一个从旋转内落包层向内盘（~30 au）过渡的结构，双星引力扰动造成盘中子结构；外流壳层的运动学特征不支持盘风起源，而更符合夹带模型。

Abstract: We present 0.1" (~ 50 au) resolution Atacama Large Millimeter/submillimeter Array (ALMA) observations of the HH 46/47 molecular outflow and its envelope-disk system. The 1.3 mm continuum emission reveals a compact central source surrounded by a circumbinary disk with substructures. The companion, identified in optical and infrared observations, is not detected in the millimeter continuum but coincides with a local intensity minimum. Two spur-like features extending from the primary source toward the companion are identified and are likely induced by gravitational perturbations from the companion. The envelope-disk system is traced by C18O, SO, H2CO, and CH3OH. C18O primarily traces the extended envelope, while SO probes the inner envelope, and H2CO and CH3OH trace compact, faster-rotating structures near the centrifugal barrier. The observations are well reproduced by a rotating-infalling envelope transitioning to an inner disk at a radius of ~30 au around a 0.3 Msun protostar. The 12CO emission, together with JWST NIRCam images, reveals multiple shell structures in the outflow. Using C18O and 13CO to correct for optical depth, we derive the spatial distributions of outflow mass, momentum, and kinetic energy, as well as their corresponding rates. A model-independent analysis of a well-defined redshifted shell yields its three-dimensional velocity field, showing that the shell expands radially rather than flowing along its surface. Although a transverse velocity gradient is detected, interpreting it as rotation implies an unphysically large magnetic lever arm, disfavoring a direct disk-wind origin. Instead, the shell kinematics support an entrainment scenario.

### [30] [A Steep-Extinction QSO at z=4.6: JWST Evidence for Abundant Small Dust Grains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02685)
*Mingyu Li,Zheng Cai,Roberto Maiolino,Fengwu Sun,Xihan Ji,Qiao Duan,Bjorn H. C. Emonts,Xiaohui Fan,Ignas Juodžbalis,Xiaojing Lin,Yixiao Liu,Sandro Tacchella*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (82/100) - 这篇论文利用JWST首次在z>4.6类星体中识别出陡峭消光曲线与缺失2175埃特征并存的独特尘埃成分，对理解早期宇宙中小颗粒硅酸盐尘埃的快速形成机制，以及修正高红移类星体光度与星族模型具有直接参考价值。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用JWST/NIRSpec光谱观测并识别出类星体UDS-27023（红移z=4.556±0.003），将其光谱与类星体复合模板进行定量比较，分析其远紫外消光曲线和2175埃特征。

Result: UDS-27023展现出极陡的远紫外消光曲线（A1500/AV≈8），但缺乏2175埃吸收特征，表明星际介质中以小尺寸硅酸盐尘埃颗粒为主导。

Conclusion: 这一现象表明类星体环境中存在活跃的小颗粒产生和加工过程。类星体驱动的激波和外流对预先存在的大颗粒进行机械破碎是一种自然途径，而类星体驱动的致密风中原位凝结硅酸盐颗粒则提供了额外可能。这类陡消光类星体可能揭示了活跃星系核生成、加工和再分布小颗粒的短寿命阶段，有助于促进星际介质中快速的晶粒生长并丰富星系周介质。

Abstract: The rapid accumulation of massive dust reservoirs in the early Universe remains a major challenge in astrophysics. While core-collapse supernovae can inject large dust grains ($a \gtrsim 0.1\,μ{\rm m}$) on short timescales, explaining the total dust budgets in the early Universe likely requires efficient grain growth in the interstellar medium (ISM). Such growth depends critically on an abundant population of small grains, which maximize the surface area available for accretion and may be generated by rapid dust-processing or dust-formation channels. Here, we report the discovery of a QSO UDS-27023 at $z=4.556\pm0.003$, identified using JWST/NIRSpec spectroscopy. By quantitatively comparing the spectra to QSO composite templates, we find that UDS-27023 displays an exceptionally steep far-UV extinction curve ($A_{1500}/A_V \approx 8$) but notably lacks the 2175 Angstrom bump, indicating a dominance of small silicate dust grains. We interpret this phenomenology as evidence for active small-grain production and processing in the QSO environment. Mechanical shattering of pre-existing large grains by QSO-driven shocks and outflows provides one natural pathway, while in-situ condensation of silicate grains inside dense QSO-driven winds may offer an additional route. Such a population of steep-extinction QSOs (SEQs) may therefore reveal a short-lived phase in which luminous AGN generate, process, and redistribute small grains, potentially facilitating rapid ISM grain growth and enriching the circumgalactic medium.

TL;DR: 基于HST、ALMA和AstroSat/UVIT的高分辨率成像观测，发现棒旋星系NGC 3351中棒状结构驱动的气体重新分布抑制了其中心区域的恒星形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用HST、ALMA和AstroSat/UVIT的高分辨率成像数据，分析NGC 3351的尘埃分布、分子气体以及恒星形成活动的空间对应关系。
